  field(SCAN, "I/O Intr")
  field(PINI, "1")
  field(TSE, "-2")
  field(DTYP, "asynFloat64")
  field(INP, "@asyn($(PORT),0,1)ADSPORT=851/POLL_RATE=1/PMPS_GVL.cstFullBeam.fAtt?")
  field(PREC, "3")
  field(EGU, "%")
  info(autosaveFields_pass0, "PREC")
  info(archive, "monitor 1: VAL")
}
